to JIT Compiled Code Chain\\n\\n## Overview\\nThe Java bytecode JIT compilation chain in OpenJDK consists of a complete pipeline that transforms bytecode into machine code and installs it into the code cache. This trace follows the C2 (HotSpot Server) compiler path.\\n\\n## Compilation Chain Flow\\n\\n### 1. CompileBroker - Compilation Request Entry Point\\n**File**: `src/hotspot/share/compiler/compileBroker.cpp` (line 1338)\\n**Symbol**: `CompileBroker::compile_method()`\\n\\nThe CompileBroker is the central dispatcher for all JIT compilation requests. It receives method compilation requests and manages compiler threads. The `compile_method()` function initiates the compilation process by creating a CompileTask and submitting it to available compiler threads.\\n\\n### 2. C2Compiler - C2 Compiler Entry Point\\n**File**: `src/hotspot/share/opto/c2compiler.cpp` (line 117)\\n**Symbol**: `C2Compiler::compile_method()`\\n\\nThe C2Compiler class implements the main C2 compilation entry point. The `compile_method()` method receives a ciEnv (compiler interface environment), the target ciMethod to compile, and compilation options. It orchestrates the entire compilation by:\\n- Setting up compilation options (escape analysis, lock elimination, etc.)\\n- Creating a Compile object which performs the actual compilation\\n- Handling compilation failures and retries with adjusted options\\n\\n### 3.
